	id = HF.20374
	hide_window = yes

	only_rulers = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
		OR = { 
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
		NOR =  { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
		}
	}
	immediate = { 
		add_trait = uncrowned
	}
}

#Five-yearly random bad events for uncrowned rulers.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20375
	hide_window = yes


	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		is_feudal = yes
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
		ruled_years = 5
		OR = { 
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
		NOR =  { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_priest
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_bishop
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_pope
			government = order_government 
		}
	}

	immediate = { 
		#Random negative flavour.
		random_list = { 
			20 = { 
				character_event = { id = HF.20376 days = 100 random = 100 } #Peasants are upset.
			}
			20 = { 
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0
					NOT	= { 
						any_vassal = { 
							is_theocracy = yes
							count = 2
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = HF.20377 days = 100 random = 100 } #Priests are upset.
			}
			20 = { 
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0
					is_married = no
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0
					spouse = { 
						NOR = { 
							religion = catholic
							religion = ursuline
							religion = mormon
							religion = high_church
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.75
					spouse = { 
						trait = wroth
					}
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.75
					spouse = { 
						OR = { 
							trait = crowned_by_priest
							trait = crowned_by_bishop
							trait = crowned_by_pope
							trait = crowned_by_myself
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.5
					spouse = { 
						higher_real_tier_than = ROOT
					}
				}
				spouse = { character_event = { id = HF.20378 days = 100 random = 100 } } #Spouse is upset.
			}
			20 = { 
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0
					NOT = { any_courtier_or_vassal = { has_job_title = job_chancellor } }
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.75
					any_courtier_or_vassal = { 
						has_job_title = job_chancellor 
						trait = wroth
					}
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = { 
					limit = { has_job_title = job_chancellor }
					character_event = { id = HF.20384 days = 100 random = 100 } #Chancellor is upset.
				} 
			}
			10 = { 
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0
					NOT = { any_courtier_or_vassal = { has_job_title = job_spiritual } }
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 0.25
					any_courtier_or_vassal = { 
						has_job_title = job_spiritual 
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.75
					any_courtier_or_vassal = { 
						has_job_title = job_spiritual 
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				modifier = { 
					factor = 1.75

					}
				}

				modifier = {

						trait = wroth
					}
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = { 
					limit = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }

				} 
			}
			10 = {

					tier = EMPEROR
				}

				#	has_landed_title = e_hre
				#}

#Generic Flavor events related to coronation and crowns.

#Peasants are restless because ruler is uncrowned.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20376
	desc = EVTDESCHFA20376

	picture = GFX_evt_peasants
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = { 
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		NOR = { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
		}
		OR = { 
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
		capital_scope = { religion = ROOT }
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHF20376
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = peasant_unrest
				duration = 365
				stacking = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 100		
		}
	}
}

#Church vassals upset because of uncrowned ruler.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20377
	desc = EVTDESCHFA20377

	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = { 
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		NOR = { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
		}
		OR = { 
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAHF20377
		trigger = { learning = 12 }
		tooltip_info = learning
		custom_tooltip = { text = tooltip_explain_coronation }
		piety = 50

#Former guest is envious of extravagant coronation.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20392
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_modifier = crowned_in_barn
		}
		text = EVTDESCHFA20392		
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = crowned_in_barn }
		}
		text = EVTDESCHFB20392		
	}

	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		FROMFROM = { has_character_modifier = extravagant_coronation }
		OR = { 
			has_character_modifier = crowned_in_barn
			NOR = { 
				trait = crowned_by_priest
				trait = crowned_by_bishop
				trait = crowned_by_pope
				trait = crowned_by_myself
			}
		}
	 } 
	option = { 
		name = EVTOPTAHF20392
		trigger = { trait = humble } 
		tooltip_info = humble
		piety = 50
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 50
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = EVTOPTBHF20392
		if = { 
			limit = { trait = kind } 
			remove_trait = kind
			break = yes
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				NOR = { 
					trait = kind 
					trait = envious
				} 
			} 
			add_trait = envious
			break = yes
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { trait = envious } 
			piety = -50
			break = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#New Vassals must pay homage to a crowned King.

#On_death event for vassal of crowned ruler.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20393
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		religion_group = christian
		is_feudal = yes 
		independent = no
		higher_real_tier_than = COUNT #Avoid spamming.
		current_heir = { age = 12 } #At the very least
		liege = { 
			NOT = { character = ROOT }
			NOT = { 
				current_heir = { character = PREV } 
			}
			NOT = { #Prevent same vassal from giving homage multiple times when inheriting new titles within the realm (from siblings and such)
				current_heir = { vassal_of = PREV } 
			}
			religion_group = christian
			higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
			OR = { 
				trait = crowned_by_priest
				trait = crowned_by_bishop
				trait = crowned_by_pope
				trait = crowned_by_myself
			}
			in_command = no
		}
	 } 

	immediate = { 
		current_heir = { character_event = { id = HF.20394 days = 4 random = 4 } }
	}
}

#Heir is prompted to go to his liege.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20394
	desc = EVTDESCHFA20394		

	picture = GFX_evt_diplomatic_greeting
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		independent = no
		age = 12
		is_feudal = yes 
		religion_group = christian
		liege = { 
			NOT = { character = ROOT }
			higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
			OR = { 
				trait = crowned_by_priest
				trait = crowned_by_bishop
				trait = crowned_by_pope
				trait = crowned_by_myself
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Will go.
		name = EVTOPTAHF20394
		prestige = -50
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = out_traveling
			duration = 50
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { liege = { character_event = { id = HF.20396 days = 25 random = 10 } } } #Liege event.

		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 80
		}
	}
	option = { #Will not go.
		name = EVTOPTBHF20394
		hidden_tooltip = { liege = { character_event = { id = HF.20395 days = 15 random = 15 } } } #Notify.

		liege = {
				show_scope_change = no	
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_didnot_pay_homage
				years = 15
				who = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				liege = { is_friend = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				liege = { is_lover = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { is_married = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				liege = { is_rival = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = stubborn
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				liege = { NOT = { religion = ROOT } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = 0 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -20 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -40 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -60 
					} 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Liege receives homage from vassal.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20396
	desc = EVTDESCHFA20396

	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
		OR = { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
		}
	}

	option = { #Accept homage
		name = EVTOPTAHF20396
		custom_tooltip = { text = tooltip_HF20396_A }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = { 
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						religion = FROM 
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_infidel
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { age = 16 }
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_child
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { FROM = { age = 50 } }
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_old
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { FROM = { is_attractive_trigger = yes } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { is_female = yes }
						prefers_men_trigger = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { is_female = no }
						prefers_men_trigger = no
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_attractive
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { FROM = { is_unattractive_trigger = yes } } 
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_deformed
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { is_female = no }
						OR = { 
							has_law = agnatic_succession
							has_law = cognatic_succession 
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						FROM = { is_female = yes }
						OR = { 
							has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
							has_law = enatic_succession 
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_sex
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { FROM = { is_evil_trigger = yes } }  
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_evil
				}
				20 = { 
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { FROM = { has_virtue_trigger = yes } }  
					}
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_good
				}
				1 = {
					set_character_flag = flag_homage_generic
				}
			} 

			character_event = { id = HF.20410 } # Reaction event.
		}
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 95
		}
	}
	option = { #Refuse homage
		name = EVTOPTBHF20396
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = HF.20398 } } } #Notify.
		prestige = 100
		FROM = {
				show_scope_change = no	
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_offended
				years = 15
				who = ROOT
			}
		} 
		ai_chance = { 	
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				liege = { is_friend = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				liege = { is_lover = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { is_married = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				liege = { is_rival = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = stubborn
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = 0 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -20 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -40 
					} 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { 
					opinion = { 
						who = FROM
						value = -60 
					} 
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#The nail in the Iron Cross. (this will never fire)
character_event = {
	id = HF.20399
	desc = EVTDESCHFA20399

	picture = GFX_evt_holy_emperor
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	ai = no
	min_age = 8

	trigger = { 	
		NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = flag_nail_in_crown }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		religion_group = christian
		any_artifact = {
			artifact_type = iron_crown_of_lombardy
			is_artifact_equipped = yes 
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = shrewd
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = dull
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { age = 16 }
		}
	}

	immediate = { set_dynasty_flag = flag_nail_in_crown }


	option = { #Look for it
		name = EVTOPTAHF20399
		change_learning = 3
		random = {
			chance = 10
			piety = -100
			custom_tooltip = { text = iron_cross_broken }
			hidden_tooltip = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = iron_crown_of_lombardy }
					unsafe_destroy_artifact = yes
					add_artifact = fragment_of_true_cross
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Better not to touch.
		name = EVTOPTBHF20399
		piety = 75
	}
}

#The HRE crown and the prince.  (this will also never fire)
character_event = {
	id = HF.20400
	hide_window = yes

	ai = no

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 	
		NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = flag_hre_crown_prince }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = is_charlemagne }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
		religion_group = christian
		has_landed_title = e_hre
		any_artifact = {
			artifact_type = crown_hre
			is_artifact_equipped = yes 
		}
		any_child = {
			is_alive = yes
			age = 7
			NOT = { age = 14 }
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
			at_location = ROOT
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			any_child = {
				is_alive = yes
				age = 7
				NOT = { age = 14 }
				NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				at_location = ROOT
				trait = curious
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_child = {
				is_alive = yes
				age = 7
				NOT = { age = 14 }
				NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
				at_location = ROOT
				trait = rowdy
			}
		}
	}


	immediate = {

				is_alive = yes
				age = 7

	}

#Thicking negative modifier for uncrowned rulers. Fired Five-Yearly.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20405
	hide_window = yes


	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		is_feudal = yes
		is_adult = yes
		is_vice_royalty = no
		NOT = { government = order_government }
		higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
		OR = { 
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
		NOT = { check_variable = { which = uncrowned_count value = 30 } } #Stop at minus thirty.
		NOR =  { 
			trait = crowned_by_priest
			trait = crowned_by_bishop
			trait = crowned_by_pope
			trait = crowned_by_myself
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_priest
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_bishop
			has_character_flag = flag_crowned_by_pope
		}
	}

	immediate = { 
		change_variable = { which = uncrowned_count value = 1 }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = uncrowned_modifier
			duration = -1
			stacking = yes
		}
	}
}

				save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_midewiwincrown
			}
			current_heir = { character_event = { id = HF.20407 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_landed_title = d_raven_tales_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_raven_tales_fylkir }
			}
			d_raven_tales_reformed = { 
				current_heir = { save_event_target_as = worthy_raven_tales_fylkir_crown }
			}
			player_heir = { save_event_target_as = unworthy_raven_tales_fylkir_crown }
			any_artifact = { 
				limit = { artifact_type = scepter_raven_tales_fylkir }
				save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_raven_talescrown
			}
			current_heir = { character_event = { id = HF.20407 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_landed_title = d_trailwalker_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir }
			}
			d_trailwalker_reformed = { 
				current_heir = { save_event_target_as = worthy_trailwalker_fylkir_crown }
			}
			player_heir = { save_event_target_as = unworthy_trailwalker_fylkir_crown }
			any_artifact = { 
				limit = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir }
				save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_trailwalkercrown
			}
			current_heir = { character_event = { id = HF.20407 days = 1 } }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_landed_title = e_california
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_california }
			}
			e_california = { 
				current_heir = { save_event_target_as = worthy_california_crown }
			}
			player_heir = { save_event_target_as = unworthy_california_crown }
			any_artifact = { 
				limit = { artifact_type = crown_california }
				save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_4
			}
			current_heir = { character_event = { id = HF.20407 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

					has_character_flag = flag_homage_seduce_failure
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_mock_failure

			}
		}
		opinion = { 
			modifier = opinion_pleased
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = HF.20412 } } } 
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_play_failure
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_seduce_failure
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_mock_failure
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_formal_failure

			text = EVTOPTBHF20411_A
			trigger = { 
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_play_success
					has_character_flag = flag_homage_seduce_success

					has_character_flag = flag_homage_formal_success

					has_character_flag = flag_homage_informal_failure
				}
			}
		}
		opinion = {

			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = HF.20413 } } }

			modifier = {

#On_title_usurped: move special crowns to new holder. FROMFROM = old holder, FROM = title, ROOT = new holder.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20414
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {	
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = e_dixie } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_hcc } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = e_california } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_california } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = e_caribbean } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_lion_judah } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_norse_pagan_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_fylkir } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_celtic_pagan_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_celtic_fylkir } } 
			}
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_espiritista_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_espiritista_fylkir } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_revelationist_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_revelationist_fylkir } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_occultist_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_occultist_fylkir } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_thelemic_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_thelemic_fylkir } } 
			} 
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_midewiwin_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_midewiwin_fylkir } } 
			}
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_raven_tales_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_raven_tales_fylkir } } 
			}
			AND = {
				FROM = { title = d_trailwalker_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir } } 
			} 
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = e_dixie } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_hcc } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_hcc }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = e_california } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_california } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_california }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_4
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = e_caribbean } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_lion_judah } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_lion_judah }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_2
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_norse_pagan_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_3
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_thelemic_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_thelemic_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_thelemic_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_thelemiccrown 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_celtic_pagan_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_celtic_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_celtic_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_celticcrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_espiritista_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_espiritista_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_espiritista_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_espiritistacrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_revelationist_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_revelationist_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_revelationist_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_revelationistcrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_occultist_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_occultist_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_occultist_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_occultistcrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_midewiwin_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_midewiwin_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = scepter_midewiwin_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_midewiwincrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_raven_tales_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_raven_tales_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = scepter_raven_tales_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_raven_talescrown
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { title = d_trailwalker_reformed } 
				FROMFROM = { any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir } } 
			} 
			FROMFROM = { 
				any_artifact = { 
					limit = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir }
					save_event_target_as = inheriting_artifact_trailwalkercrown
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_1 = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		} 
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_2 = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_3 = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_thelemiccrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_celticcrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_espiritistacrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_revelationistcrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_occultistcrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_rust_cultistcrown = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		}
		event_target:inheriting_artifact_4 = {
			transfer_artifact = {
				from = FROMFROM
				to = ROOT
 			} 
 		} 
	}
}

#On_death: add special dead_crown trait to make the dead Emperors wear their special crowns even after they've given up the artifact itself.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20415
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { 
		has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		OR =  { 
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_dixie
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_hcc } 
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_caribbean 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_lion_judah }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_norse_pagan_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_celtic_pagan_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_celtic_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_espiritista_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_espiritista_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_revelationist_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_revelationist_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_occultist_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_occultist_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_thelemic_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_thelemic_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_midewiwin_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_midewiwin_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_raven_tales_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_raven_tales_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_trailwalker_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir }
			}
			AND =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_california
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_california }
			}
		#	AND =  { 
		#		has_landed_title = k_italy 
		#		any_artifact = { artifact_type = iron_crown_of_lombardy }
		#	}
		#	AND =  { 
		#		any_artifact = { artifact_type = cursed_diamond_crown }
		#	}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_dixie
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_hcc }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_hcc
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_caribbean
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_lion_judah }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_judah
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_norse_pagan_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_celtic_pagan_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_celtic_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_celtic_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_espiritista_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_espiritista_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_espiritista_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_revelationist_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_revelationist_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_revelationist_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_occultist_pagan_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_occultist_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_occultist_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_thelemic_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_thelemic_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_thelemic_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_midewiwin_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_midewiwin_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_scepter_midewiwin_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_raven_tales_reformed
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = scepter_raven_tales_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_raven_tales_fylkir
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = e_california
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_california }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_california
		}
		if =  { 
			limit =  { 
				has_landed_title = d_trailwalker_reformed 
				any_artifact = { artifact_type = crown_trailwalker_fylkir }
			}
			add_trait = dead_crown_trailwalker_fylkir
		}
		#if =  { 
		#	limit =  { 
		#		has_landed_title = k_italy 
		#		any_artifact = { artifact_type = iron_crown_of_lombardy }
		#	}
		#	add_trait = dead_iron_crown_lombardy
		#}
	}
}
#On_conversion: clean up uncrowned modifier.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20416
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = uncrowned_modifier
		NOR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = ursuline
			religion = mormon
			religion = high_church
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifiers = { modifier = uncrowned_modifier amount = 30 } 	
		set_variable = { which = uncrowned_count value = 0 }
	}
}
#On_new_holder: clean up uncrowned modifier. FROMFROM = Title's old holder.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20417
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROMFROM = {
			has_character_modifier = uncrowned_modifier
			NOT = { #If no longer King-tier.
				higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = { 
			remove_character_modifiers = { modifier = uncrowned_modifier amount = 30 } 
			set_variable = { which = uncrowned_count value = 0 }
		} 	
	}
}

#Check edge cases of a ruler's heir inheriting a _for_coronation flag when the war itself is about to be invalidated for whatever reason.
character_event = {
	id = HF.20418
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	has_character_flag = flag_antipope_for_coronation 

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			any_war = {
				using_cb = depose_antipope
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = flag_antipope_for_coronation 
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = HF.20419
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	has_character_flag = flag_excommunicated_for_coronation  

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			lower_real_tier_than = KING
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					using_cb = excommunicated_ruler
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = flag_excommunicated_for_coronation 
	}
}
